--In-Game Trades--
Trading ABRA for MIMIEN the MR. MIME has become trading ABRA for MIMIEN the LUDICOLO
Trading POLIWHIRL for ZYNX the JYNX has become trading POLIWHIRL for ZYNX the SKITTY
Trading NIDORAN♂ for MS. NIDO the NIDORAN♀ has become trading NIDORAN♂ for MS. NIDO the STARYU
Trading SPEAROW for CH’DING the FARFETCH’D has become trading SPEAROW for CH’DING the REGIROCK
Trading NIDORINO for NINA the NIDORINA has become trading NIDORINO for NINA the SLAKOTH

Trading RAICHU for ESPHERE the ELECTRODE has become trading RAICHU for ESPHERE the SUDOWOODO
